{\footnotesize\ttfamily collator\+\_\+compare (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{class_collator}{Collator}}}]{\$object,  }\item[{}]{\$str1,  }\item[{}]{\$str2 }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

(P\+HP 5 $>$= 5.\+3.\+0, P\+E\+CL intl $>$= 1.\+0.\+0)~\newline
 Compare two Unicode strings \mbox{\hyperlink{patch2_8txt_a3f9992ab8fa942ed02faa63682c3a84c}{Collator \$object  string \$str1 }} The first string to compare. 


\begin{DoxyParams}[1]{Parameters}
string & {\em \$str2} & \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
The second string to compare. 

\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
int Return comparison result\+:
\end{DoxyReturn}


1 if {\itshape str1} is greater than {\itshape str2} ; 

0 if {\itshape str1} is equal to {\itshape str2}; 

-\/1 if {\itshape str1} is less than {\itshape str2} . 

On error boolean {\bfseries{F\+A\+L\+SE}} is returned. \mbox{\Hypertarget{intl_8php_a8f964e6e55c94a9cd44668553da616c9}\label{intl_8php_a8f964e6e55c94a9cd44668553da616c9}}

 Create a collator \mbox{\hyperlink{patch2_8txt_a3f9992ab8fa942ed02faa63682c3a84c}{string \$locale }} The locale containing the required collation rules. Special values for locales can be passed in -\/ if null is passed for the locale, the default locale collation rules will be used. If empty string (\char`\"{}\char`\"{}) or \char`\"{}root\char`\"{} are passed, U\+CA rules will be used.

{\footnotesize\ttfamily datefmt\+\_\+format\+\_\+object (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{}]{\$object,  }\item[{}]{\$format = {\ttfamily NULL},  }\item[{}]{\$locale = {\ttfamily NULL} }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

(P\+HP 5 $>$= 5.\+5.\+0, P\+E\+CL intl $>$= 3.\+0.\+0)~\newline
 Formats an object \mbox{\hyperlink{patch2_8txt_a3f9992ab8fa942ed02faa63682c3a84c}{object \$object }} An object of type \mbox{\hyperlink{class_intl_calendar}{Intl\+Calendar}} or \mbox{\hyperlink{class_date_time}{Date\+Time}}. The timezone information in the object will be used. 


\begin{DoxyParams}[1]{Parameters}
mixed & {\em \$format} & \mbox{[}optional\mbox{]} \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
How to format the date/time. This can either be an \{\href{https://secure.php.net/manual/en/language.types.array.php}{\texttt{ https\+://secure.\+php.\+net/manual/en/language.\+types.\+array.\+php}} array\} with two elements (first the date style, then the time style, these being one of the constants {\bfseries{\mbox{\hyperlink{class_intl_date_formatter_ac62f1cfad2f7d0988d46057bf55d1e80}{Intl\+Date\+Formatter\+::\+N\+O\+NE}}}}, {\bfseries{\mbox{\hyperlink{class_intl_date_formatter_a7c5b0c14382692b4f858ae0e29abc6be}{Intl\+Date\+Formatter\+::\+S\+H\+O\+RT}}}}, {\bfseries{\mbox{\hyperlink{class_intl_date_formatter_a7ca655183eb9a4bd8ae93d82c64209b8}{Intl\+Date\+Formatter\+::\+M\+E\+D\+I\+UM}}}}, {\bfseries{\mbox{\hyperlink{class_intl_date_formatter_aee6315761c9eccd7954a29c1d070c7a5}{Intl\+Date\+Formatter\+::\+L\+O\+NG}}}}, {\bfseries{\mbox{\hyperlink{class_intl_date_formatter_acd6dd9fdad4996fa7c449d4d9e18a23f}{Intl\+Date\+Formatter\+::\+F\+U\+LL}}}}), a long with the value of one of these constants (in which case it will be used both for the time and the date) or a \mbox{\hyperlink{patch2_8txt_a3f9992ab8fa942ed02faa63682c3a84c}{https\+://secure.\+php.\+net/manual/en/language.\+types.\+string.\+php}} with the format described in \mbox{\hyperlink{}{the I\+CU documentation}} documentation. If {\bfseries{N\+U\+LL}}, the default style will be used. 


\begin{DoxyParams}[1]{Parameters}
string | null & {\em \$locale} & \mbox{[}optional\mbox{]} \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
The locale to use, or N\+U\+LL to use the default one.

string$\vert$false The formatted string or, if an error occurred, {\bfseries{F\+A\+L\+SE}}. 
\end{DoxyReturn}

{\footnotesize\ttfamily datefmt\+\_\+parse (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{class_message_formatter}{Message\+Formatter}}}]{\$mf,  }\item[{}]{\$value,  }\item[{\&}]{\$position = {\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{_core__d_8php_afa4c647ecaee0da639b8549bb3abf62b}{null}}} }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

(P\+HP 5 $>$= 5.\+3.\+0, P\+E\+CL intl $>$= 1.\+0.\+0)~\newline
 Parse string to a timestamp value \mbox{\hyperlink{patch2_8txt_a3f9992ab8fa942ed02faa63682c3a84c}{Message\+Formatter \$mf  string \$value }} string to convert to a time 


\begin{DoxyParams}[1]{Parameters}
int & {\em \$position} & \mbox{[}optional\mbox{]} \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
Position at which to start the parsing in \$value (zero-\/based). If no error occurs before \$value is consumed, \$parse\+\_\+pos will contain -\/1 otherwise it will contain the position at which parsing ended (and the error occurred). This variable will contain the end position if the parse fails. If \$parse\+\_\+pos $>$ strlen(\$value), the parse fails immediately. 

\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
int timestamp parsed value 
\end{DoxyReturn}

\index{intl.php@{intl.php}!datefmt\_set\_timezone@{datefmt\_set\_timezone}}
\index{datefmt\_set\_timezone@{datefmt\_set\_timezone}!intl.php@{intl.php}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{datefmt\_set\_timezone()}{datefmt\_set\_timezone()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily datefmt\+\_\+set\+\_\+timezone (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{class_message_formatter}{Message\+Formatter}}}]{\$mf,  }\item[{}]{\$zone }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

(P\+HP 5 $>$= 5.\+5.\+0, P\+E\+CL intl $>$= 3.\+0.\+0)~\newline
 Sets formatter\textquotesingle{}s timezone \mbox{\hyperlink{patch2_8txt_a3f9992ab8fa942ed02faa63682c3a84c}{Message\+Formatter \$mf  mixed \$zone }} The timezone to use for this formatter. This can be specified in the following forms\+: 
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item 

{\bfseries{N\+U\+LL}}, in which case the default timezone will be used, as specified in the ini setting \mbox{\hyperlink{}{date.\+timezone}} or through the function \mbox{\hyperlink{}{date\+\_\+default\+\_\+timezone\+\_\+set()}} and as returned by \mbox{\hyperlink{}{date\+\_\+default\+\_\+timezone\+\_\+get()}}. 


\item 

An \mbox{\hyperlink{}{Intl\+Time\+Zone}}, which will be used directly. 


\item 

\mbox{\hyperlink{class_a}{A}} \mbox{\hyperlink{}{Date\+Time\+Zone}}. Its identifier will be extracted and an I\+CU timezone object will be created; the timezone will be backed by I\+CU\textquotesingle{}s database, not P\+HP\textquotesingle{}s. 


\item 

\mbox{\hyperlink{class_a}{A}} \mbox{\hyperlink{}{string}}, which should be a valid I\+CU timezone identifier. See {\bfseries{\mbox{\hyperlink{class_intl_time_zone_af956faf07a5114e8eee1826aae88ac2b}{Intl\+Time\+Zone\+::create\+Time\+Zone\+I\+D\+Enumeration()}}}}. Raw offsets such as {\itshape \char`\"{}\+G\+M\+T+08\+:30\char`\"{}} are also accepted. 


\end{DoxyItemize}

\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
bool {\bfseries{T\+R\+UE}} on success or {\bfseries{F\+A\+L\+SE}} on failure. 
\end{DoxyReturn}
\mbox{\Hypertarget{intl_8php_ad0b68e773d34171870af16d5fef7bbf3}\label{intl_8php_ad0b68e773d34171870af16d5fef7bbf3}}

\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{grapheme\_extract()}{grapheme\_extract()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily grapheme\+\_\+extract (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{}]{\$haystack,  }\item[{}]{\$size,  }\item[{}]{\$extract\+\_\+type = {\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{_core__d_8php_afa4c647ecaee0da639b8549bb3abf62b}{null}}},  }\item[{}]{\$start = {\ttfamily 0},  }\item[{\&}]{\$next = {\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{_core__d_8php_afa4c647ecaee0da639b8549bb3abf62b}{null}}} }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

(P\+HP 5 $>$= 5.\+3.\+0, P\+E\+CL intl $>$= 1.\+0.\+0)~\newline
 Function to extract a sequence of default grapheme clusters from a text buffer, which must be encoded in U\+T\+F-\/8. \mbox{\hyperlink{patch2_8txt_a3f9992ab8fa942ed02faa63682c3a84c}{string \$haystack }} String to search. 


\begin{DoxyParams}[1]{Parameters}
int & {\em \$size} & \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
Maximum number items -\/ based on the \$extract\+\_\+type -\/ to return. 


\begin{DoxyParams}[1]{Parameters}
int & {\em \$extract\+\_\+type} & \mbox{[}optional\mbox{]} \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
Defines the type of units referred to by the \$size parameter\+: 

G\+R\+A\+P\+H\+E\+M\+E\+\_\+\+E\+X\+T\+R\+\_\+\+C\+O\+U\+NT (default) -\/ \$size is the number of default grapheme clusters to extract. G\+R\+A\+P\+H\+E\+M\+E\+\_\+\+E\+X\+T\+R\+\_\+\+M\+A\+X\+B\+Y\+T\+ES -\/ \$size is the maximum number of bytes returned. G\+R\+A\+P\+H\+E\+M\+E\+\_\+\+E\+X\+T\+R\+\_\+\+M\+A\+X\+C\+H\+A\+RS -\/ \$size is the maximum number of U\+T\+F-\/8 characters returned. 


\begin{DoxyParams}[1]{Parameters}
int & {\em \$start} & \mbox{[}optional\mbox{]} \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
Starting position in \$haystack in bytes -\/ if given, it must be zero or a positive value that is less than or equal to the length of \$haystack in bytes. If \$start does not point to the first byte of a U\+T\+F-\/8 character, the start position is moved to the next character boundary. 


\begin{DoxyParams}[1]{Parameters}
int & {\em \$next} & \mbox{[}optional\mbox{]} \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
Reference to a value that will be set to the next starting position. When the call returns, this may point to the first byte position past the end of the string. 

\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
string$\vert$false \mbox{\hyperlink{class_a}{A}} string starting at offset \$start and ending on a default grapheme cluster boundary that conforms to the \$size and \$extract\+\_\+type specified. 
\end{DoxyReturn}

int & {\em \$offset} & \mbox{[}optional\mbox{]} \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
The optional \$offset parameter allows you to specify where in \$haystack to start searching as an offset in grapheme units (not bytes or characters). The position returned is still relative to the beginning of haystack regardless of the value of \$offset. 

\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
int$\vert$false the position as an integer. If needle is not found, \mbox{\hyperlink{standard__1_8php_a75b50139ee3829fbfd47af6805284786}{strpos()}} will return boolean F\+A\+L\+SE. 
\end{DoxyReturn}

\index{grapheme\_substr@{grapheme\_substr}!intl.php@{intl.php}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{grapheme\_substr()}{grapheme\_substr()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily grapheme\+\_\+substr (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{}]{\$string,  }\item[{}]{\$start,  }\item[{}]{\$length = {\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{_core__d_8php_afa4c647ecaee0da639b8549bb3abf62b}{null}}} }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

(P\+HP 5 $>$= 5.\+3.\+0, P\+E\+CL intl $>$= 1.\+0.\+0)~\newline
 Return part of a string \mbox{\hyperlink{patch2_8txt_a3f9992ab8fa942ed02faa63682c3a84c}{string \$string }} The input string. Must be valid U\+T\+F-\/8. 


\begin{DoxyParams}[1]{Parameters}
int & {\em \$start} & \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
Start position in default grapheme units. If \$start is non-\/negative, the returned string will start at the \$start\textquotesingle{}th position in \$string, counting from zero. If \$start is negative, the returned string will start at the \$start\textquotesingle{}th grapheme unit from the end of string. 


\begin{DoxyParams}[1]{Parameters}
int & {\em \$length} & \mbox{[}optional\mbox{]} \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
Length in grapheme units. If \$length is given and is positive, the string returned will contain at most \$length grapheme units beginning from \$start (depending on the length of string). If \$length is given and is negative, then that many grapheme units will be omitted from the end of string (after the start position has been calculated when a start is negative). If \$start denotes a position beyond this truncation, {\bfseries{F\+A\+L\+SE}} will be returned. 

\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
string$\vert$false 
\end{DoxyReturn}
the extracted part of \$string,~\newline
 or {\bfseries{F\+A\+L\+SE}} if \$length is negative and \$start denotes a position beyond truncation \$length,~\newline
 or also {\bfseries{F\+A\+L\+SE}} if \$start denotes a position beyond \$string length\mbox{\Hypertarget{intl_8php_ad214fdc7e75000129257c9ffc2b4a351}\label{intl_8php_ad214fdc7e75000129257c9ffc2b4a351}} 
\index{intl.php@{intl.php}!idn\_to\_ascii@{idn\_to\_ascii}}
\index{idn\_to\_ascii@{idn\_to\_ascii}!intl.php@{intl.php}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{idn\_to\_ascii()}{idn\_to\_ascii()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily idn\+\_\+to\+\_\+ascii (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{}]{\$domain,  }\item[{}]{\$options = {\ttfamily 0},  }\item[{}]{\$variant = {\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{intl_8php_a8c83a4515e86c861310a15aed0fbc687}{I\+N\+T\+L\+\_\+\+I\+D\+N\+A\+\_\+\+V\+A\+R\+I\+A\+N\+T\+\_\+2003}}},  }\item[{array \&}]{\$idna\+\_\+info }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

(P\+HP 5 $>$= 5.\+3.\+0, P\+HP 7, P\+E\+CL intl $>$= 1.\+0.\+2, P\+HP 7, P\+E\+CL idn $>$= 0.\+1)~\newline
 Convert domain name to I\+D\+NA A\+S\+C\+II form. \mbox{\hyperlink{patch2_8txt_a3f9992ab8fa942ed02faa63682c3a84c}{string \$domain }} Domain to convert. In P\+HP 5 must be U\+T\+F-\/8 encoded. If e.\+g. an I\+S\+O-\/8859-\/1 (aka Western Europe latin1) encoded string is passed it will be converted into an A\+CE encoded \char`\"{}xn-\/-\/\char`\"{} string. It will not be the one you expected though! 


\begin{DoxyParams}[1]{Parameters}
int & {\em \$options} & \mbox{[}optional\mbox{]} \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
Conversion options -\/ combination of I\+D\+N\+A\+\_\+$\ast$ constants (except I\+D\+N\+A\+\_\+\+E\+R\+R\+O\+R\+\_\+$\ast$ constants). 


\begin{DoxyParams}[1]{Parameters}
int & {\em \$variant} & \mbox{[}optional\mbox{]} \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
Either I\+N\+T\+L\+\_\+\+I\+D\+N\+A\+\_\+\+V\+A\+R\+I\+A\+N\+T\+\_\+2003 for I\+D\+NA 2003 or I\+N\+T\+L\+\_\+\+I\+D\+N\+A\+\_\+\+V\+A\+R\+I\+A\+N\+T\+\_\+\+U\+T\+S46 for U\+TS \#46. 


\begin{DoxyParams}[1]{Parameters}
array & {\em \$idna\+\_\+info} & \mbox{[}optional\mbox{]} \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
This parameter can be used only if I\+N\+T\+L\+\_\+\+I\+D\+N\+A\+\_\+\+V\+A\+R\+I\+A\+N\+T\+\_\+\+U\+T\+S46 was used for variant. In that case, it will be filled with an array with the keys \textquotesingle{}result\textquotesingle{}, the possibly illegal result of the transformation, \textquotesingle{}is\+Transitional\+Different\textquotesingle{}, a boolean indicating whether the usage of the transitional mechanisms of U\+TS \#46 either has or would have changed the result and \textquotesingle{}errors\textquotesingle{}, which is an int representing a bitset of the error constants I\+D\+N\+A\+\_\+\+E\+R\+R\+O\+R\+\_\+$\ast$. 

\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
string$\vert$false The A\+CE encoded version of the domain name or {\bfseries{F\+A\+L\+SE}} on failure. 
\end{DoxyReturn}
\mbox{\Hypertarget{intl_8php_ae348d11fb425aba08c637313c9547419}\label{intl_8php_ae348d11fb425aba08c637313c9547419}}

(P\+HP 5 $>$= 5.\+3.\+0, P\+HP 7, P\+E\+CL intl $>$= 1.\+0.\+2, P\+HP 7, P\+E\+CL idn $>$= 0.\+1)~\newline
 Convert domain name from I\+D\+NA A\+S\+C\+II to Unicode. \mbox{\hyperlink{patch2_8txt_a3f9992ab8fa942ed02faa63682c3a84c}{string \$domain }} Domain to convert in I\+D\+NA A\+S\+C\+I\+I-\/compatible format. \end{DoxyParams}

\end{DoxyParams}

\begin{DoxyParams}[1]{Parameters}

In that case, it will be filled with an array with the keys \textquotesingle{}result\textquotesingle{}, the possibly illegal result of the transformation, \textquotesingle{}is\+Transitional\+Different\textquotesingle{}, a boolean indicating whether the usage of the transitional mechanisms of U\+TS \#46 either has or would have changed the result and \textquotesingle{}errors\textquotesingle{}, which is an int representing a bitset of the error constants I\+D\+N\+A\+\_\+\+E\+R\+R\+O\+R\+\_\+$\ast$. 

\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
string$\vert$false The U\+T\+F-\/8 encoded version of the domain name or {\bfseries{F\+A\+L\+SE}} on failure. R\+FC 3490 4.\+2 states though \char`\"{}\+To\+Unicode never fails. If any step fails, then the original input
sequence is returned immediately in that step.\char`\"{} 
\end{DoxyReturn}

\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{intlcal\_add()}{intlcal\_add()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily intlcal\+\_\+add (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{}]{\$calendar,  }\item[{}]{\$field,  }\item[{}]{\$amount }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

(P\+HP 5 $>$=5.\+5.\+0 P\+E\+CL intl $>$= 3.\+0.\+0a1)~\newline
 Add a (signed) amount of time to a field \mbox{\hyperlink{patch2_8txt_a3f9992ab8fa942ed02faa63682c3a84c}{Intl\+Calendar \$calendar }} The calendar object, on the procedural style interface. 


\begin{DoxyParams}[1]{Parameters}
int & {\em \$field} & \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
One of the \mbox{\hyperlink{patch2_8txt_a3f9992ab8fa942ed02faa63682c3a84c}{Intl\+Calendar}} date/time \mbox{\hyperlink{}{field constants}}. These are integer values between {\itshape 0} and {\bfseries{Intl\+Calendar\+::\+F\+I\+E\+L\+D\+\_\+\+C\+O\+U\+NT}}. 


\begin{DoxyParams}[1]{Parameters}
int & {\em \$amount} & \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
The signed amount to add to the current field. If the amount is positive, the instant will be moved forward; if it is negative, the instant wil be moved into the past. The unit is implicit to the field type. For instance, hours for \mbox{\hyperlink{class_intl_calendar_a16a5ecdaed4825b224bbd6fb5453719a}{Intl\+Calendar\+::\+F\+I\+E\+L\+D\+\_\+\+H\+O\+U\+R\+\_\+\+O\+F\+\_\+\+D\+AY}}.

\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
bool Returns {\bfseries{T\+R\+UE}} on success or {\bfseries{F\+A\+L\+SE}} on failure. 
\end{DoxyReturn}

\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{intlcal\_create\_instance()}{intlcal\_create\_instance()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily intlcal\+\_\+create\+\_\+instance (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{}]{\$time\+Zone = {\ttfamily NULL},  }\item[{}]{\$locale = {\ttfamily NULL} }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

(P\+HP 5 $>$=5.\+5.\+0 P\+E\+CL intl $>$= 3.\+0.\+0a1)~\newline
 Create a new \mbox{\hyperlink{class_intl_calendar}{Intl\+Calendar}} \mbox{\hyperlink{patch2_8txt_a3f9992ab8fa942ed02faa63682c3a84c}{mixed \$time\+Zone \mbox{[}optional\mbox{]} }} 

The timezone to use. 


\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item 

{\bfseries{N\+U\+LL}}, in which case the default timezone will be used, as specified in the ini setting \mbox{\hyperlink{}{date.\+timezone}} or through the function \mbox{\hyperlink{patch2_8txt_a3f9992ab8fa942ed02faa63682c3a84c}{date\+\_\+default\+\_\+timezone\+\_\+set()}} and as returned by \mbox{\hyperlink{patch2_8txt_a3f9992ab8fa942ed02faa63682c3a84c}{date\+\_\+default\+\_\+timezone\+\_\+get()}}. 


\item 

An \mbox{\hyperlink{patch2_8txt_a3f9992ab8fa942ed02faa63682c3a84c}{Intl\+Time\+Zone}}, which will be used directly. 


\item 

\mbox{\hyperlink{class_a}{A}} \mbox{\hyperlink{patch2_8txt_a3f9992ab8fa942ed02faa63682c3a84c}{Date\+Time\+Zone}}. Its identifier will be extracted and an I\+CU timezone object will be created; the timezone will be backed by I\+CU\textquotesingle{}s database, not P\+HP\textquotesingle{}s. 


\item 

\mbox{\hyperlink{class_a}{A}} \mbox{\hyperlink{patch2_8txt_a3f9992ab8fa942ed02faa63682c3a84c}{string}}, which should be a valid I\+CU timezone identifier. See {\bfseries{\mbox{\hyperlink{class_intl_time_zone_af956faf07a5114e8eee1826aae88ac2b}{Intl\+Time\+Zone\+::create\+Time\+Zone\+I\+D\+Enumeration()}}}}. Raw offsets such as {\itshape \char`\"{}\+G\+M\+T+08\+:30\char`\"{}} are also accepted. 


\end{DoxyItemize}


\begin{DoxyParams}[1]{Parameters}
string & {\em \$locale} & \mbox{[}optional\mbox{]} \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\mbox{\hyperlink{class_a}{A}} locale to use or {\bfseries{N\+U\+LL}} to use \mbox{\hyperlink{}{the default locale}}. 

\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
\mbox{\hyperlink{class_intl_calendar}{Intl\+Calendar}} The created \mbox{\hyperlink{patch2_8txt_a3f9992ab8fa942ed02faa63682c3a84c}{Intl\+Calendar}} instance or {\bfseries{N\+U\+LL}} on failure. 
\end{DoxyReturn}

 Compare time of two \mbox{\hyperlink{class_intl_calendar}{Intl\+Calendar}} objects for equality \mbox{\hyperlink{patch2_8txt_a3f9992ab8fa942ed02faa63682c3a84c}{Intl\+Calendar \$calendar\+Object }} The calendar object, on the procedural style interface.

\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
bool 
\end{DoxyReturn}
Returns {\bfseries{T\+R\+UE}} if the current time of both this and the passed in \mbox{\hyperlink{patch2_8txt_a3f9992ab8fa942ed02faa63682c3a84c}{Intl\+Calendar}} object are the same, or {\bfseries{F\+A\+L\+SE}} otherwise. In any case, the two cases can be distinguished by calling \mbox{\hyperlink{patch2_8txt_a3f9992ab8fa942ed02faa63682c3a84c}{intl\+\_\+get\+\_\+error\+\_\+code()}}. \mbox{\Hypertarget{intl_8php_a44fdb897c066f54f6e2389d4134e76eb}\label{intl_8php_a44fdb897c066f54f6e2389d4134e76eb}}

\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
Whether to fetch the actual locale (the locale from which the calendar data originates, with {\bfseries{\mbox{\hyperlink{class_locale_aa318f27d34790e49b2e86174e101ac5a}{Locale\+::\+A\+C\+T\+U\+A\+L\+\_\+\+L\+O\+C\+A\+LE}}}}) or the valid locale, i.\+e., the most specific locale supported by I\+CU relatively to the requested locale  see {\bfseries{\mbox{\hyperlink{class_locale_a2f835518e2e2449788915c12ce30eb56}{Locale\+::\+V\+A\+L\+I\+D\+\_\+\+L\+O\+C\+A\+LE}}}}. \begin{DoxyItemize}
\item 

{\bfseries{N\+U\+LL}}, in which case the default timezone will be used, as specified in the ini setting \mbox{\hyperlink{}{date.\+timezone}} or through the function \mbox{\hyperlink{patch2_8txt_a3f9992ab8fa942ed02faa63682c3a84c}{date\+\_\+default\+\_\+timezone\+\_\+set()}} and as returned by \mbox{\hyperlink{patch2_8txt_a3f9992ab8fa942ed02faa63682c3a84c}{date\+\_\+default\+\_\+timezone\+\_\+get()}}. 


\item 

An \mbox{\hyperlink{patch2_8txt_a3f9992ab8fa942ed02faa63682c3a84c}{Intl\+Time\+Zone}}, which will be used directly. 


\item 

\mbox{\hyperlink{class_a}{A}} \mbox{\hyperlink{patch2_8txt_a3f9992ab8fa942ed02faa63682c3a84c}{Date\+Time\+Zone}}. Its identifier will be extracted and an I\+CU timezone object will be created; the timezone will be backed by I\+CU\textquotesingle{}s database, not P\+HP\textquotesingle{}s. 


\item 

\mbox{\hyperlink{class_a}{A}} \mbox{\hyperlink{patch2_8txt_a3f9992ab8fa942ed02faa63682c3a84c}{string}}, which should be a valid I\+CU timezone identifier. See {\bfseries{\mbox{\hyperlink{class_intl_time_zone_af956faf07a5114e8eee1826aae88ac2b}{Intl\+Time\+Zone\+::create\+Time\+Zone\+I\+D\+Enumeration()}}}}. Raw offsets such as {\itshape \char`\"{}\+G\+M\+T+08\+:30\char`\"{}} are also accepted. 


\end{DoxyItemize}\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
bool Returns {\bfseries{T\+R\+UE}} on success and {\bfseries{F\+A\+L\+SE}} on failure. 
\end{DoxyReturn}
\mbox{\Hypertarget{intl_8php_ad7dda2700e88557cbdf1100d07a36233}\label{intl_8php_ad7dda2700e88557cbdf1100d07a36233}}

{\footnotesize\ttfamily intlcal\+\_\+to\+\_\+date\+\_\+time (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{}]{\$calendar }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

(P\+HP 5 $>$=5.\+5.\+0 P\+E\+CL intl $>$= 3.\+0.\+0a2)~\newline
 Convert an \mbox{\hyperlink{class_intl_calendar}{Intl\+Calendar}} into a \mbox{\hyperlink{class_date_time}{Date\+Time}} object \mbox{\hyperlink{patch2_8txt_a3f9992ab8fa942ed02faa63682c3a84c}{Intl\+Calendar \$calendar }} The calendar object, on the procedural style interface. 

\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
Date\+Time$\vert$false \mbox{\hyperlink{class_a}{A}} \mbox{\hyperlink{patch2_8txt_a3f9992ab8fa942ed02faa63682c3a84c}{Date\+Time}} object with the same timezone as this object (though using P\+HP\textquotesingle{}s database instead of I\+CU\textquotesingle{}s) and the same time, except for the smaller precision (second precision instead of millisecond). Returns {\bfseries{F\+A\+L\+SE}} on failure. 
\end{DoxyReturn}

\index{locale\_compose@{locale\_compose}!intl.php@{intl.php}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{locale\_compose()}{locale\_compose()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily locale\+\_\+compose (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{array}]{\$subtags }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

(P\+HP 5 $>$= 5.\+3.\+0, P\+E\+CL intl $>$= 1.\+0.\+0)~\newline
 Returns a correctly ordered and delimited locale ID \mbox{\hyperlink{patch2_8txt_a3f9992ab8fa942ed02faa63682c3a84c}{array \$subtags }} an array containing a list of key-\/value pairs, where the keys identify the particular locale ID subtags, and the values are the associated subtag values. 

The \textquotesingle{}variant\textquotesingle{} and \textquotesingle{}private\textquotesingle{} subtags can take maximum 15 values whereas \textquotesingle{}extlang\textquotesingle{} can take maximum 3 values.\+e.\+g. Variants are allowed with the suffix ranging from 0-\/14. Hence the keys for the input array can be variant0, variant1, ...,variant14. In the returned locale id, the subtag is ordered by suffix resulting in variant0 followed by variant1 followed by variant2 and so on. 

The \textquotesingle{}variant\textquotesingle{}, \textquotesingle{}private\textquotesingle{} and \textquotesingle{}extlang\textquotesingle{} multiple values can be specified both as array under specific key (e.\+g. \textquotesingle{}variant\textquotesingle{}) and as multiple numbered keys (e.\+g. \textquotesingle{}variant0\textquotesingle{}, \textquotesingle{}variant1\textquotesingle{}, etc.). 

\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
string The corresponding locale identifier. 
\end{DoxyReturn}

(P\+HP 5 $>$= 5.\+3.\+0, P\+E\+CL intl $>$= 1.\+0.\+0)~\newline
 Searches the language tag list for the best match to the language \mbox{\hyperlink{patch2_8txt_a3f9992ab8fa942ed02faa63682c3a84c}{array \$langtag }} An array containing a list of language tags to compare to {\itshape locale}. Maximum 100 items allowed.

\end{DoxyParams}

\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{locale\_parse()}{locale\_parse()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily locale\+\_\+parse (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{}]{\$locale }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

(P\+HP 5 $>$= 5.\+3.\+0, P\+E\+CL intl $>$= 1.\+0.\+0)~\newline
 Returns a key-\/value array of locale ID subtag elements. \mbox{\hyperlink{patch2_8txt_a3f9992ab8fa942ed02faa63682c3a84c}{string \$locale }} The locale to extract the subtag array from. Note\+: The \textquotesingle{}variant\textquotesingle{} and \textquotesingle{}private\textquotesingle{} subtags can take maximum 15 values whereas \textquotesingle{}extlang\textquotesingle{} can take maximum 3 values. 

\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
array an array containing a list of key-\/value pairs, where the keys identify the particular locale ID subtags, and the values are the associated subtag values. The array will be ordered as the locale id subtags e.\+g. in the locale id if variants are \textquotesingle{}-\/var\+X-\/var\+Y-\/varZ\textquotesingle{} then the returned array will have variant0=$>$varX , variant1=$>$varY , variant2=$>$varZ 
\end{DoxyReturn}

\index{transliterator\_transliterate@{transliterator\_transliterate}!intl.php@{intl.php}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{transliterator\_transliterate()}{transliterator\_transliterate()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily transliterator\+\_\+transliterate (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{}]{\$transliterator,  }\item[{}]{\$subject,  }\item[{}]{\$start = {\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{_core__d_8php_afa4c647ecaee0da639b8549bb3abf62b}{null}}},  }\item[{}]{\$end = {\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{_core__d_8php_afa4c647ecaee0da639b8549bb3abf62b}{null}}} }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

(P\+HP $>$= 5.\+4.\+0, P\+E\+CL intl $>$= 2.\+0.\+0)~\newline
 Transliterate a string \mbox{\hyperlink{patch2_8txt_a3f9992ab8fa942ed02faa63682c3a84c}{Transliterator$\vert$string \$transliterator  string \$subject }} The string to be transformed. 


\begin{DoxyParams}[1]{Parameters}
int & {\em \$start} & \mbox{[}optional\mbox{]} \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
The start index (in U\+T\+F-\/16 code units) from which the string will start to be transformed, inclusive. Indexing starts at 0. The text before will be left as is. 


\begin{DoxyParams}[1]{Parameters}
int & {\em \$end} & \mbox{[}optional\mbox{]} \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
The end index (in U\+T\+F-\/16 code units) until which the string will be transformed, exclusive. Indexing starts at 0. The text after will be left as is. 

\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
string$\vert$false The transfomed string on success, or {\bfseries{F\+A\+L\+SE}} on failure. 
\end{DoxyReturn}
